</div>
			<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Deaths in 2015</h1>
									<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
									<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
								<div id="contentSub"></div>
												<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
				</div>
				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><p>This is a chronology of <b>deaths in 2015</b>. Names are reported under the date of death. Names under each date are reported in alphabetical order by family name or <a href="/wiki/Pseudonym" title="Pseudonym">pseudonym</a>. Deaths of non-humans are reported here if they first have their own Wikipedia article. Notable persons without an article can be listed for one month after death to prompt creation of one. A typical entry reports information in the following sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>Name, age, country of citizenship at birth, subsequent country of citizenship (if applicable), reason for notability, cause of death (if known) and reference.</li>
</ul>
<div style="clear: right; margin-bottom: .5em; float: right; padding: .5em 0 .8em 1.4em; background: none; width: auto;">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="16"><a href="/wiki/October_16" title="October 16">16</a></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Luciano_Garc%C3%ADa_Al%C3%A9n" title="Luciano García Alén">Luciano García Alén</a>, 87, Spanish physician and ethnographer.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ralph_Andrews" title="Ralph Andrews">Ralph Andrews</a>, 87, American television producer (<i><a href="/wiki/You_Don%27t_Say!" title="You Don't Say!">You Don't Say!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Liar%27s_Club" title="Liar's Club">Liar's Club</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Lingo_(U.S._game_show)" title="Lingo (U.S. game show)">Lingo</a></i>), Alzheimer's disease.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bevo_(mascot)" title="Bevo (mascot)">Bevo XIV</a>, 13, American longhorn steer collegiate mascot (<a href="/wiki/University_of_Texas_at_Austin" title="University of Texas at Austin">Texas Longhorns</a>), bovine leukemia virus.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Francesc_de_Paula_Burguera" title="Francesc de Paula Burguera">Francesc de Paula Burguera</a>, 87, Spanish journalist and politician, member of the <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Deputies_(Spain)" title="Congress of Deputies (Spain)">Congress of Deputies</a> (1977–1979).<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Burtsev" title="Mikhail Burtsev">Mikhail Burtsev</a>, 59, Russian Soviet fencer, six-time world champion, two-time Olympic champion (<a href="/wiki/Fencing_at_the_1976_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_team_sabre" title="Fencing at the 1976 Summer Olympics – Men's team sabre">1976</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fencing_at_the_1980_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_team_sabre" title="Fencing at the 1980 Summer Olympics – Men's team sabre">1980</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span>[</span>31<span>]</span></a></sup></li>

<li id="cite_note-346"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-346">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.20min.ch/ro/sports/football/story/Jean-Jacques-Tillmann-est-decede-28370804">Jean-Jacques Tillmann est décédé</a> <span class="languageicon" style="font-size:0.95em; font-weight:bold; color:#555;">(French)</span></span></li>
